These cells are slender bipolar cells of the developing marginal zone. One feature of these cells in mammals is that they express the Reelin gene."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

#### Added
- [Cajal-Retzius cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000695) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "CR cells" 

- [Cajal-Retzius cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000695) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A neuron of the human embryonic marginal zone which display, as a salient feature, radial ascending processes that contact the pial surface, and a horizontal axon plexus located in the deep marginal zone. One feature of these cells in mammals is that they express the Reelin gene." 

- [Cajal-Retzius cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000695) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "While previously called 'pioneer neurons' of the marginal zone, Cajal-Retzius cells are differentiated from pioneer neurons (which are Reln-negative) by their Reln-immunoreactivity." 

- [Cajal-Retzius cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000695) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "Horizontal cells of Cajal"

### Chandelier Pvalb GABAergic cortical interneuron `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023036`
#### Removed
- [Chandelier Pvalb GABAergic cortical interneuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023036) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "Chandelier PV (Mus)"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [Chandelier Pvalb GABAergic cortical interneuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023036) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "Chandelier Pvalb GABAergic cortical interneuron (Mus musculus)"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [Chandelier Pvalb GABAergic cortical interneuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023036) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A Pvalb GABAergic cortical interneuron that is recognizable by the straight terminal axonal 'cartridges' of vertically oriented strings of synaptic boutons. Chandelier PV cells have soma found in in upper L2/3, with some in deep L5. Chandelier PV cells exhibit fast-spiking but lower firing rate compared to basket cells, and have practically absent hyperpolarization sag. Chandelier PV cells' boutons target exclusively the axon initial segment (AIS) of pyramidal cells, with a single cell innervating hundreds of pyramidal cells in a clustered manner."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

#### Added
- [Chandelier Pvalb GABAergic cortical interneuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023036) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "Chandelier PV" 

- [Chandelier Pvalb GABAergic cortical interneuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023036) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A Pvalb GABAergic cortical interneuron that is recognizable by the straight terminal axonal 'cartridges' of vertically oriented strings of synaptic boutons. Chandelier PV cells' boutons target exclusively the axon initial segment (AIS) of pyramidal cells, with a single cell innervating hundreds of pyramidal cells in a clustered manner." 

- [Chandelier Pvalb GABAergic cortical interneuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023036) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "Chandelier Pvalb GABAergic cortical interneuron" 

- [Chandelier Pvalb GABAergic cortical interneuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023036) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "In mice, Chandelier PV cells have soma found in in upper L2/3, with some in deep L5 and exhibit fast-spiking but lower firing rate compared to basket cells, and have practically absent hyperpolarization sag."

If in doubt, please consider using CL:0002489 'double negative thymocyte'."

### L5 T-Martinotti Sst GABAergic cortical interneuron (Mus musculus) `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023027`
#### Removed
- [L5 T-Martinotti Sst GABAergic cortical interneuron (Mus musculus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023027) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A Sst GABAergic cortical interneuron with a soma found in L5 and possesses 'T-shaped' martinotti morphologies with local axonal plexus in L5a and translaminar axons restricted to the uppermost part of L1. They show low-threshold spiking patterns with strong rebound firing, and inhibit the L1 apical tuft of nearby pyramidal cells."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

#### Added

They show low-threshold spiking patterns with strong rebound firing, and inhibit the L1 apical tuft of nearby pyramidal cells."

- [Mueller cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000636) SubClassOf [astrocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000127) 

#### Added
- [Mueller cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000636) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "M&uuml;ller cell" 

- [Mueller cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000636) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "Astrocyte-like radial glial cell that extends vertically throughout the retina, with the nucleus are usually in the middle of the inner nuclear layer." 

- [Mueller cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000636) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "Muller glia" 

- [Mueller cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000636) SubClassOf [radial glial cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000681) 

- [Mueller cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000636) SubClassOf [retinal cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009004)

#### Added
- [in_left_side_of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BSPO_0000120)(?y, ?z), [part_of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000050)(?x, ?y) -> [in_left_side_of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BSPO_0000120)(?x, ?z) 
  - [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "This can't be added as a property chain because it causes a circularity violation for 'part of'." 

- [in_right_side_of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BSPO_0000121)(?y, ?z), [part_of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000050)(?x, ?y) -> [in_right_side_of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BSPO_0000121)(?x, ?z) 
  - [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "This can't be added as a property chain because it causes a circularity violation for 'part of'." 

- [in lateral side of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BSPO_0000126)(?y, ?z), [part_of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000050)(?x, ?y) -> [in lateral side of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BSPO_0000126)(?x, ?z)

### alpha7 GABAergic cortical interneuron (Mus musculus) `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023010`
#### Removed
- [alpha7 GABAergic cortical interneuron (Mus musculus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023010) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "A7 cells have a transcriptomics signature that looks like Lamp5 GABAergic interneuron."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [alpha7 GABAergic cortical interneuron (Mus musculus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023010) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "Unlike typical Lamp5 electrophysiology, A7 cells have Vip- and Sst-like firing properties, with active depolarizing hump at near-threshold membrane potentials, and  larger hyperpolarization sag, stronger burst, and rebound firing."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

#### Added
- [alpha7 GABAergic cortical interneuron (Mus musculus)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023010) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "Unlike typical Lamp5 electrophysiology, A7 cells have Vip- and Sst-like firing properties, with active depolarizing hump at near-threshold membrane potentials, and  larger hyperpolarization sag, stronger burst, and rebound firing. A7 cells have a transcriptomics signature that looks like Lamp5 GABAergic interneuron."

- [arachnoid barrier cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023097) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "AB cell" 

- [arachnoid barrier cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023097) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "ABC" 

- [arachnoid barrier cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023097) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A mesothelial fibroblast of the arachnoid barrier layer. Arachnoid barrier cells make up the tight-junctioned layer in the leptomeninx that functions as the physiologic barrier between the cerebrospinal fluid in the subarachnoid space and the fenestrated capillaries in the dura." 

- [arachnoid barrier cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023097) [creator](http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/creator) [0000-0001-7258-9596](http://orcid.org/0000-0001-7258-9596)

### cnidocyte `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0011029`

#### Added
- [cnidocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0011029) [created_by](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#created_by) "http://orcid.org/0000-0001-5208-3432"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [cnidocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0011029) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "cnidocyte" 

- [cnidocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0011029) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "An explosive cell containing one giant secretory organelle called a cnidocyst (also known as a cnida (plural cnidae) or nematocyst) that contains a toxin responsible for the stings delivered by a cnidarian to other organisms. Cnidae are used to capture prey and as a defense against predators. The presence of cnidocytes defines the phylum Cnidaria (corals, sea anemones, hydrae, jellyfish, etc.)." 

- [cnidocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0011029) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "cnidoblast" 

- [cnidocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0011029) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "nematocyte" 

- [cnidocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0011029) [id](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#id) "CL:0011029"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

### continuant `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000002`
#### Removed
- [continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000002) SubClassOf [part_of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000050) only [continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000002) 

#### Added
- [continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000002) [IAO_0000600](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000600) "A continuant is an entity that persists, endures, or continues to exist through time while maintaining its identity. (axiom label in BFO2 Reference: [008-002])"@en 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [008-002](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/008-002) 

- [continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000002) [isDefinedBy](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#isDefinedBy) [bfo.owl](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo.owl) 

- [continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000002) [BFO_0000180](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000180) "Continuant" 

- [continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000002) [IAO_0000602](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000602) "(forall (x) (if (Continuant x) (Entity x))) // axiom label in BFO2 CLIF: [008-002] " 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [008-002](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/008-002) 

- [continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000002) [IAO_0000602](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000602) "(forall (x y) (if (and (Continuant x) (exists (t) (hasContinuantPartOfAt y x t))) (Continuant y))) // axiom label in BFO2 CLIF: [126-001] " 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [126-001](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/126-001) 

- [continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000002) [IAO_0000601](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000601) "if b is a continuant and if, for some t, cis continuant_part of b at t, then c is a continuant. (axiom label in BFO2 Reference: [009-002])"@en 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [009-002](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/009-002) 

- [continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000002) [IAO_0000602](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000602) "(forall (x) (if (Material Entity x) (exists (t) (and (TemporalRegion t) (existsAt x t))))) // axiom label in BFO2 CLIF: [011-002] " 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [011-002](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/011-002) 

- [continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000002) [editor note](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000116) "Continuant doesn't have a closure axiom because the subclasses don't necessarily exhaust all possibilites. For example, in an expansion involving bringing in some of Ceuster's other portions of reality, questions are raised as to whether universals are continuants"@en 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [0000007](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/0000007) 

- [continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000002) [IAO_0000601](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000601) "if b is a material entity, then there is some temporal interval (referred to below as a one-dimensional temporal region) during which b exists. (axiom label in BFO2 Reference: [011-002])"@en 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [011-002](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/011-002) 

- [continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000002) [IAO_0000602](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000602) "(forall (x y) (if (and (Continuant x) (exists (t) (continuantPartOfAt y x t))) (Continuant y))) // axiom label in BFO2 CLIF: [009-002] " 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [009-002](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/009-002) 

- [continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000002) [BFO_0000179](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000179) "continuant" 

- [continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000002) [IAO_0000601](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000601) "if b is a continuant and if, for some t, c has_continuant_part b at t, then c is a continuant. (axiom label in BFO2 Reference: [126-001])"@en 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [126-001](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/126-001) 

- [continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000002) [editor note](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000116) "BFO 2 Reference: Continuant entities are entities which can be sliced to yield parts only along the spatial dimension, yielding for example the parts of your table which we call its legs, its top, its nails. &lsquo;My desk stretches from the window to the door. It has spatial parts, and can be sliced (in space) in two. With respect to time, however, a thing is a continuant.&rsquo; [60, p. 240"@en

### displaced amacrine cell `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023119`

#### Added
- [displaced amacrine cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023119) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "Displaced amacrine cells are a subset of Sox2 expressing amacrine cells." 

- [displaced amacrine cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023119) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "dACs" 

- [displaced amacrine cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023119) [id](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#id) "CL:4023119"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [displaced amacrine cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023119) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A subpopulation of amacrine cell that migrate further than other amacrine cells, and come to lie basal to the inner plexiform layer (IPL) in the ganglion cell layer. Displaced amacrine cells still have their neurites extending apically into the IPL, and therefore exhibit an inverted polarity with respect to the other amacrine cells." 

- [displaced amacrine cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023119) [creator](http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/creator) [0000-0001-7258-9596](http://orcid.org/0000-0001-7258-9596) 

- [displaced amacrine cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023119) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "displaced amacrine cell" 

- [displaced amacrine cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023119) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "inverted amacrine cell" 

- Class: [displaced amacrine cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023119) 

- [displaced amacrine cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023119) SubClassOf [amacrine cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000561)

### disposition `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000016`

#### Added
- [disposition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000016) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "children are innately disposed to categorize objects in certain ways."@en 

- [disposition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000016) [IAO_0000600](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000600) "b is a disposition means: b is a realizable entity &amp; b&rsquo;s bearer is some material entity &amp; b is such that if it ceases to exist, then its bearer is physically changed, &amp; b&rsquo;s realization occurs when and because this bearer is in some special physical circumstances, &amp; this realization occurs in virtue of the bearer&rsquo;s physical make-up. (axiom label in BFO2 Reference: [062-002])"@en 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [062-002](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/062-002) 

- [disposition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000016) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "disposition"@en 

- [disposition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000016) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "certain people have a predisposition to colon cancer"@en 

- [disposition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000016) [BFO_0000179](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000179) "disposition" 

- [disposition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000016) [BFO_0000180](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000180) "Disposition"

  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [062-002](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/062-002) 

- [disposition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000016) [editor note](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000116) "BFO 2 Reference: Dispositions exist along a strength continuum. Weaker forms of disposition are realized in only a fraction of triggering cases. These forms occur in a significant number of cases of a similar type."@en 

- [disposition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000016) [IAO_0000602](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000602) "(forall (x t) (if (and (RealizableEntity x) (existsAt x t)) (exists (y) (and (MaterialEntity y) (specificallyDepends x y t))))) // axiom label in BFO2 CLIF: [063-002] " 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [063-002](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/063-002) 

- [disposition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000016) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "the cell wall is disposed to filter chemicals in endocytosis and exocytosis"@en 

- [disposition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000016) [IAO_0000601](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000601) "If b is a realizable entity then for all t at which b exists, b s-depends_on some material entity at t. (axiom label in BFO2 Reference: [063-002])"@en 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [063-002](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/063-002) 

- [disposition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000016) [isDefinedBy](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#isDefinedBy) [bfo.owl](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo.owl) 

- [disposition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000016) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "an atom of element X has the disposition to decay to an atom of element Y"@en

### entity `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000001`

#### Added
- [entity](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000001) [BFO_0000180](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000180) "Entity" 

- [entity](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000001) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "the Second World War"@en 

- [entity](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000001) [editor note](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000116) "BFO 2 Reference: In all areas of empirical inquiry we encounter general terms of two sorts. First are general terms which refer to universals or types:animaltuberculosissurgical procedurediseaseSecond, are general terms used to refer to groups of entities which instantiate a given universal but do not correspond to the extension of any subuniversal of that universal because there is nothing intrinsic to the entities in question by virtue of which they &ndash; and only they &ndash; are counted as belonging to the given group. Examples are: animal purchased by the Emperortuberculosis diagnosed on a Wednesdaysurgical procedure performed on a patient from Stockholmperson identified as candidate for clinical trial #2056-555person who is signatory of Form 656-PPVpainting by Leonardo da VinciSuch terms, which represent what are called &lsquo;specializations&rsquo; in [81"@en 

- [entity](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000001) [IAO_0000600](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000600) "An entity is anything that exists or has existed or will exist. (axiom label in BFO2 Reference: [001-001])"@en 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [001-001](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/001-001) 

- [entity](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000001) [isDefinedBy](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#isDefinedBy) [bfo.owl](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo.owl) 

- [entity](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000001) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "Verdi&rsquo;s Requiem"@en 

- [entity](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000001) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "Julius Caesar"@en 

- [entity](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000001) [BFO_0000179](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000179) "entity" 

- [entity](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000001) [editor note](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000116) "Entity doesn't have a closure axiom because the subclasses don't necessarily exhaust all possibilites. For example Werner Ceusters 'portions of reality' include 4 sorts, entities (as BFO construes them), universals, configurations, and relations. It is an open question as to whether entities as construed in BFO will at some point also include these other portions of reality. See, for example, 'How to track absolutely everything' at http://www.referent-tracking.com/_RTU/papers/CeustersICbookRevised.pdf"@en 
  - [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "per discussion with Barry Smith" 

  - [see also](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso) [CeustersICbookRevised.pdf](http://www.referent-tracking.com/_RTU/papers/CeustersICbookRevised.pdf) 

  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [0000004](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/0000004) 

- [entity](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000001) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "your body mass index"@en

### function `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000034`

#### Added
- [function](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000034) [IAO_0000602](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000602) "(forall (x) (if (Function x) (Disposition x))) // axiom label in BFO2 CLIF: [064-001] "

- [function](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000034) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "the function of amylase in saliva to break down starch into sugar"@en 

- [function](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000034) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "the function of a heart pacemaker to regulate the beating of a heart through electricity"@en 

- [function](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000034) [IAO_0000600](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000600) "A function is a disposition that exists in virtue of the bearer&rsquo;s physical make-up and this physical make-up is something the bearer possesses because it came into being, either through evolution (in the case of natural biological entities) or through intentional design (in the case of artifacts), in order to realize processes of a certain sort. (axiom label in BFO2 Reference: [064-001])"@en 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [064-001](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/064-001) 

- [function](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000034) [BFO_0000180](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000180) "Function" 

- [function](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000034) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "function"@en 

- [function](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000034) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "the function of a hammer to drive in nails"@en 

- [function](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000034) [BFO_0000179](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000179) "function" 

- [function](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000034) [editor note](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000116) "BFO 2 Reference: In the past, we have distinguished two varieties of function, artifactual function and biological function. These are not asserted subtypes of BFO:function however, since the same function &ndash; for example: to pump, to transport &ndash; can exist both in artifacts and in biological entities. The asserted subtypes of function that would be needed in order to yield a separate monoheirarchy are not artifactual function, biological function, etc., but rather transporting function, pumping function, etc."@en

### lymph node mantle zone B cell `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009037`

#### Added
- [lymph node mantle zone B cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009037) [id](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#id) "CL:0009037"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [lymph node mantle zone B cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009037) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A B lymphocyte that resides in the mantle zone of the lymph node germinal center. These are generally IgM and IgD positive activated B cells that form a 'corona' around the germinal center and are part of the establishment of a secondary lymphatic follicule." 

- [lymph node mantle zone B cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009037) [has_broad_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasBroadSynonym) "mantle zone B cell" 

- [lymph node mantle zone B cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009037) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "mantle zone B cell of lymph node" 

- [lymph node mantle zone B cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009037) [created_by](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#created_by) "http://orcid.org/0000-0002-2825-0621"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [lymph node mantle zone B cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009037) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "lymph node mantle zone B cell" 

- [lymph node mantle zone B cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009037) [in_subset](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#inSubset) [location_grouping](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/cl#location_grouping) 

- Class: [lymph node mantle zone B cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009037) 

- [lymph node mantle zone B cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009037) SubClassOf [B cell](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000236)

### lymphocyte of small intestine lamina propria `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009044`

#### Added
- [lymphocyte of small intestine lamina propria](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009044) [id](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#id) "CL:0009044"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [lymphocyte of small intestine lamina propria](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009044) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A lymphocyte that resides in the lamina propria of the small intestine. Lamina propria leukocytes and intraepithelial lymphocytes are the effector compartments of the gut mucosal immune system. Lymphocytes circulate through gut associated lymphoid tissues until recruitment by intestinal antigens. They are involved in the gut immune response." 

- [lymphocyte of small intestine lamina propria](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009044) [has_broad_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasBroadSynonym) "small intestine lamina propria leukocyte" 

- [lymphocyte of small intestine lamina propria](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009044) [has_exact_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasExactSynonym) "small intestine lamina propria lymphocyte" 

- [lymphocyte of small intestine lamina propria](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009044) [in_subset](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#inSubset) [location_grouping](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/cl#location_grouping) 

- [lymphocyte of small intestine lamina propria](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009044) [has_broad_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasBroadSynonym) "gastrointestinal tract small intestine (lamina propria) leukocyte" 

- [lymphocyte of small intestine lamina propria](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009044) [has_broad_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasBroadSynonym) "small intestine lamina propria leukocyte (LPL)"

### lysosome-rich enterocyte `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0011032`

#### Added
- [lysosome-rich enterocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0011032) [has_broad_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasBroadSynonym) "vacuolated enterocyte" 

- [lysosome-rich enterocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0011032) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "An enterocyte that possesses a large supranuclear vacuolar system that preferentially internalizes dietary protein via receptor-mediated and fluid-phase endocytosis for intracellular digestion and trans-cellular transport. In zebrafish these cells are located in the posterior region of the mid intestine throughout life. In mammals they are found in the ileum pre-weaning and later are replaced by mature enterocytes." 

- [lysosome-rich enterocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0011032) [id](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#id) "CL:0011032"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

### ready for release `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000122`

#### Added
- [ready for release](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000122) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "ready for release"@en 

- [ready for release](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000122) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "Class has undergone final review, is ready for use, and will be included in the next release. Any class lacking &quot;ready_for_release&quot; should be considered likely to change place in hierarchy, have its definition refined, or be obsoleted in the next release.  Those classes deemed &quot;ready_for_release&quot; will also derived from a chain of ancestor classes that are also &quot;ready_for_release.&quot;"@en 

- Individual: [ready for release](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000122) 


### realizable entity `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000017`

- [realizable entity](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000017) [IAO_0000600](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000600) "To say that b is a realizable entity is to say that b is a specifically dependent continuant that inheres in some independent continuant which is not a spatial region and is of a type instances of which are realized in processes of a correlated type. (axiom label in BFO2 Reference: [058-002])"@en 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [058-002](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/058-002)

  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [060-002](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/060-002)

  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [058-002](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/058-002)

- [rearranging double negative thymocyte (Homo sapiens)](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009083) [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "There is growing evidence that molecular markers characterizing double negative thymocytes are different across species, especially in human versus mouse thymus. ### role `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000023`

#### Added
- [role](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000023) [IAO_0000600](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000600) "b is a role means: b is a realizable entity &amp; b exists because there is some single bearer that is in some special physical, social, or institutional set of circumstances in which this bearer does not have to be&amp; b is not such that, if it ceases to exist, then the physical make-up of the bearer is thereby changed. (axiom label in BFO2 Reference: [061-001])"@en 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [061-001](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/061-001) 

- [role](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000023) [editor note](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000116) "BFO 2 Reference: One major family of examples of non-rigid universals involves roles, and ontologies developed for corresponding administrative purposes may consist entirely of representatives of entities of this sort. Thus &lsquo;professor&rsquo;, defined as follows,b instance_of professor at t =Def. there is some c, c instance_of professor role &amp; c inheres_in b at t.denotes a non-rigid universal and so also do &lsquo;nurse&rsquo;, &lsquo;student&rsquo;, &lsquo;colonel&rsquo;, &lsquo;taxpayer&rsquo;, and so forth. (These terms are all, in the jargon of philosophy, phase sortals.) By using role terms in definitions, we can create a BFO conformant treatment of such entities drawing on the fact that, while an instance of professor may be simultaneously an instance of trade union member, no instance of the type professor role is also (at any time) an instance of the type trade union member role (any more than any instance of the type color is at any time an instance of the type length).If an ontology of employment positions should be defined in terms of roles following the above pattern, this enables the ontology to do justice to the fact that individuals instantiate the corresponding universals &ndash;  professor, sergeant, nurse &ndash; only during certain phases in their lives."@en 

- [role](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000023) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "the student role"@en 

- [role](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000023) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "role"@en 

- [role](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000023) [BFO_0000179](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000179) "role" 

- [role](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000023) [BFO_0000180](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000180) "Role" 

- [role](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000023) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "John&rsquo;s role of husband to Mary is dependent on Mary&rsquo;s role of wife to John, and both are dependent on the object aggregate comprising John and Mary as member parts joined together through the relational quality of being married."@en 

- [role](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000023) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "the priest role"@en 

- [role](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000023) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "the role of subject in a clinical trial"@en 

- [role](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000023) [isDefinedBy](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#isDefinedBy) [bfo.owl](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo.owl) 

- [role](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000023) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "the role of a building in serving as a military target"@en 

- [role](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000023) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "the role of a boundary to demarcate two neighboring administrative territories"@en 

- [role](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000023) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "the role of a stone in marking a property boundary"@en 

- [role](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000023) [IAO_0000602](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000602) "(forall (x) (if (Role x) (RealizableEntity x))) // axiom label in BFO2 CLIF: [061-001] " 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [061-001](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/061-001)

### spatial region `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000006`

#### Added
- [spatial region](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000006) [IAO_0000601](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000601) "All continuant parts of spatial regions are spatial regions.&nbsp;(axiom label in BFO2 Reference: [036-001])"@en 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [036-001](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/036-001) 

- [spatial region](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000006) [BFO_0000180](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000180) "SpatialRegion" 

- [spatial region](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000006) [IAO_0000602](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000602) "(forall (x) (if (SpatialRegion x) (Continuant x))) // axiom label in BFO2 CLIF: [035-001] " 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [035-001](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/035-001) 

- [spatial region](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000006) [IAO_0000602](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000602) "(forall (x y t) (if (and (SpatialRegion x) (continuantPartOfAt y x t)) (SpatialRegion y))) // axiom label in BFO2 CLIF: [036-001] " 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [036-001](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/036-001) 

- [spatial region](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000006) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "spatial region"@en 

- [spatial region](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000006) [IAO_0000600](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000600) "A spatial region is a continuant entity that is a continuant_part_of spaceR as defined relative to some frame R. (axiom label in BFO2 Reference: [035-001])"@en 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [035-001](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/035-001) 

- [spatial region](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000006) [isDefinedBy](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#isDefinedBy) [bfo.owl](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo.owl) 

- [spatial region](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000006) [BFO_0000179](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000179) "s-region" 

- [spatial region](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000006) [editor note](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000116) "Spatial region doesn't have a closure axiom because the subclasses don't exhaust all possibilites. An example would be the union of a spatial point and a spatial line that doesn't overlap the point, or two spatial lines that intersect at a single point. In both cases the resultant spatial region is neither 0-dimensional, 1-dimensional, 2-dimensional, or 3-dimensional."@en 
  - [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "per discussion with Barry Smith" 

  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [0000002](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/0000002) 

- [spatial region](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000006) [editor note](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000116) "BFO 2 Reference: Spatial regions do not participate in processes."@en 

- [spatial region](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000006) SubClassOf [immaterial entity](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000141)

### specifically dependent continuant `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000020`
#### Removed
- [specifically dependent continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000020) SubClassOf [part_of](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000050) only [specifically dependent continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000020) 

#### Added
- [specifically dependent continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000020) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "Reciprocal specifically dependent continuants: the function of this key to open this lock and the mutually dependent disposition of this lock: to be opened by this key"@en 

- [specifically dependent continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000020) [editor note](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000116) "Specifically dependent continuant doesn't have a closure axiom because the subclasses don't necessarily exhaust all possibilites. We're not sure what else will develop here, but for example there are questions such as what are promises, obligation, etc."@en 
  - [comment](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#comment) "per discussion with Barry Smith" 

  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [0000005](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/0000005) 

- [specifically dependent continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000020) [IAO_0000602](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000602) "(iff (SpecificallyDependentContinuant a) (and (Continuant a) (forall (t) (if (existsAt a t) (exists (b) (and (IndependentContinuant b) (not (SpatialRegion b)) (specificallyDependsOnAt a b t))))))) // axiom label in BFO2 CLIF: [050-003] " 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [050-003](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/050-003) 

- [specifically dependent continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000020) [BFO_0000179](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000179) "sdc" 

- [specifically dependent continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000020) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "the shape of this hole."@en 

- [specifically dependent continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000020) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "of one-sided specifically dependent continuants: the mass of this tomato"@en 

- [specifically dependent continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000020) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "the mutual dependence of proton donors and acceptors in chemical reactions [79"@en 

- [specifically dependent continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000020) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "b is a specifically dependent continuant = Def. b is a continuant &amp; there is some independent continuant c which is not a spatial region and which is such that b s-depends_on c at every time t during the course of b&rsquo;s existence. (axiom label in BFO2 Reference: [050-003])"@en 
  - [IAO_0010000](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0010000) [050-003](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/bfo/axiom/050-003)

- [specifically dependent continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000020) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "the disposition of this fish to decay"@en 

- [specifically dependent continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000020) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "of relational dependent continuants (multiple bearers): John&rsquo;s love for Mary, the ownership relation between John and this statue, the relation of authority between John and his subordinates."@en 

- [specifically dependent continuant](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/BFO_0000020) [example of usage](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000112) "the mutual dependence of the role predator and the role prey as played by two organisms in a given interaction"@en

- [transit amplifying cell of colon](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009011) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "A rapidly proliferating population of cells that differentiate from stem cells of the intestinal crypt of the large intestine. Stem cells located in the crypts of Lieberk&uuml;hn give rise to proliferating progenitor or transit amplifying cells that differentiate into the four major epithelial cell types. These include columnar absorptive cells or enterocytes, mucous secreting goblet cells, enteroendocrine cells and paneth cells."^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

### vacuolated fetal-type enterocyte `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009067`

#### Added
- [vacuolated fetal-type enterocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009067) [created_by](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#created_by) "http://orcid.org/0000-0002-2825-0621"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [vacuolated fetal-type enterocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009067) [id](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#id) "CL:0009067"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [vacuolated fetal-type enterocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009067) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "vacuolated fetal-type enterocyte" 

- [vacuolated fetal-type enterocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009067) [has_broad_synonym](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasBroadSynonym) "vacuolated enterocyte" 

- [vacuolated fetal-type enterocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009067) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "An enterocyte found in the small intestine of newborn mammals and characterized by the presence of an apical canalicular system (ACS) leading to production of large vacuoles, important for colostral macromolecule uptake. After birth, the vacuolated fetal-type enterocytes are replaced with enterocytes lacking an ACS." 

- Class: [vacuolated fetal-type enterocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009067) 

- [vacuolated fetal-type enterocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009067) SubClassOf [enterocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000584) 

- [vacuolated fetal-type enterocyte](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0009067) SubClassOf [epithelial cell of small intestine](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0002254)

### vestibular afferent neuron `http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023112`

#### Added
- [vestibular afferent neuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023112) [id](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#id) "CL:4023112"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [vestibular afferent neuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023112) [definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115) "An afferent neuron of the vestibular system that innervate the base of the hair cell and increase or decrease their neural firing rate as the receptor cell is excited or inhibited." 

- [vestibular afferent neuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023112) [label](http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label) "vestibular afferent neuron" 

- [vestibular afferent neuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023112) [creator](http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/creator) [0000-0001-7258-9596](http://orcid.org/0000-0001-7258-9596) 

- Class: [vestibular afferent neuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023112) 

- [vestibular afferent neuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_4023112) SubClassOf [sensory neuron](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/CL_0000101)
